@Override\\n94:     public void processBarrier(\\n95:             CheckpointBarrier receivedBarrier, InputChannelInfo channelInfo, boolean isRpcTriggered)\\n96:             throws IOException {\\n97: Received barrier from channel 0 (2 in total) and start a new checkpoint.\\n102:         // 2. Received EndOfPartition from channel 0.\\n103:         // 3.   int pos = 0;\\n119: \\n120:         for (CheckpointBarrierCount next : pendingCheckpoints) {\\n121:             if (next.checkpointId() == barrierId) {\\n122:                 barrierCount = and all all prior pending\\n134:                 // checkpoints (which are now subsumed)\\n135:                 for (int i = 0; i <= pos; i++) {\\n136:                     pendingCheckpoints.pollFirst();\\n137:                 }\\n138: \\n139:                 // notify the listener\\n140:                 if (!barrierCount.isAborted()) {\\n141: latestPendingCheckpointID = barrierId;\\n152:                 pendingCheckpoints.addLast(\\n153:                         new CheckpointBarrierCount(receivedBarrier, channelInfo, Flink Checkpoint Coordination Architecture\n\n## Files Examined\n\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CheckpointCoordinator.java` — JobManager-side coordinator: triggers checkpoints, collects acknowledgements, drives PendingCheckpoint → CompletedCheckpoint lifecycle\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/PendingCheckpoint.java` — In-flight checkpoint tracking: holds notYetAcknowledgedTasks, accumulates subtask states, checks isFullyAcknowledged()\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CompletedCheckpoint.java` — Finalized, persisted checkpoint containing all operator states after full acknowledgement\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/executiongraph/Execution.java` — Per-execution RPC dispatch: Execution.triggerCheckpoint() → TaskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint()\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/io/network/api/CheckpointBarrier.java` — Network event carrying checkpointId, timestamp, and CheckpointOptions propagated through operator graph\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/tasks/StreamTask.java` — Task runtime: receives RPC, calls performCheckpoint() → subtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState(); also implements triggerCheckpointOnBarrier() and abortCheckpointOnBarrier()\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/tasks/SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java` — Task-local checkpoint orchestration: broadcasts barrier downstream, calls takeSnapshotSync (operatorChain.snapshotState()), then finishAndReportAsync (AsyncCheckpointRunnable)\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/CheckpointBarrierHandler.java` — Abstract base for barrier handling: notifyCheckpoint() → toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier(), notifyAbort()\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.java` — Aligned and unaligned checkpoint barrier handler: tracks a single in-flight checkpoint, blocks channels (aligned) or passes through (unaligned), uses BarrierHandlerState state machine\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/CheckpointBarrierTracker.java` — At-least-once barrier handler: tracks barriers across multiple concurrent checkpoint IDs, does not block channels\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/CheckpointedInputGate.java` — Wraps InputGate; intercepts incoming CheckpointBarrier events and delegates to CheckpointBarrierHandler\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/InputProcessorUtil.java` — Factory that creates CheckpointBarrierHandler (SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler or CheckpointBarrierTracker) and wraps it in CheckpointedInputGate\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/io/checkpointing/BarrierHandlerState.java` — State machine interface for SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler; implementations: WaitingForFirstBarrier, AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrier, AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/CheckpointCoordinatorGateway.java` — RPC interface on JobManager accepting acknowledgeCheckpoint / declineCheckpoint from TaskManagers\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/taskmanager/RuntimeEnvironment.java` — Task-side environment: acknowledgeCheckpoint() sends AcknowledgeCheckpoint RPC message back to JobManager\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/OperatorCoordinatorCheckpoints.java` — Coordinates operator-coordinator checkpointing in parallel with task checkpointing\n- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/runtime/checkpoint/DefaultCheckpointPlanCalculator.java` — Computes which tasks trigger, which wait-for-ack, and which commit\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Entry point**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:573` — `triggerCheckpoint(boolean isPeriodic)` is called periodically by a scheduled timer (or externally for savepoints).\n\n2. **Request routing**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:626` — `chooseRequestToExecute(request).ifPresent(this::startTriggeringCheckpoint)` queues or immediately executes the trigger request through `CheckpointRequestDecider`.\n\n3. **Plan calculation**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:642` — `checkpointPlanCalculator.calculateCheckpointPlan()` (`DefaultCheckpointPlanCalculator`) determines `tasksToTrigger` (sources), `tasksToWaitFor` (all tasks needing to ack), and `tasksToCommitTo`.\n\n4. **PendingCheckpoint creation**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:901` — `createPendingCheckpoint(...)` instantiates a `PendingCheckpoint` with the set `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` from the plan, schedules a timeout canceller, and inserts it into `pendingCheckpoints` map.\n\n5. **Coordinator & master hook snapshots**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:708,736` — `OperatorCoordinatorCheckpoints.triggerAndAcknowledgeAllCoordinatorCheckpointsWithCompletion(...)` and `snapshotMasterState(checkpoint)` run asynchronously before task triggers.\n\n6. **RPC dispatch to source tasks**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:858,864` — `triggerTasks()` iterates `checkpoint.getCheckpointPlan().getTasksToTrigger()` and calls `execution.triggerCheckpoint(checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)`.\n\n7. **RPC to TaskManager**: `Execution.java:1096` — `slot.getTaskManagerGateway().triggerCheckpoint(attemptId, jobId, checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)` — actual RPC message to the remote TaskManager.\n\n8. **Task receives trigger**: `StreamTask.java:1459` — `performCheckpoint()` → `subtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState(checkpointMetaData, checkpointOptions, checkpointMetrics, operatorChain, ...)`.\n\n9. **Barrier broadcast** (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:333,344`):\n   - Step 1: `operatorChain.prepareSnapshotPreBarrier(checkpointId)` — pre-barrier operator work\n   - Step 2: `operatorChain.broadcastEvent(new CheckpointBarrier(id, ts, options), isUnaligned)` — injects barrier into output buffers, flowing downstream through the network\n\n10. **Barrier reception at downstream task**: `CheckpointedInputGate` intercepts `CheckpointBarrier` from `InputGate` and calls `barrierHandler.processBarrier(barrier, channelInfo, false)`.\n\n11. **Barrier alignment / tracking** (two implementations):\n    - **`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()`** (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.java:214`) — For exactly-once: tracks aligned channels; for aligned mode, blocks channels after first barrier (backpressure); for unaligned mode triggers immediately on first barrier announcement. Uses `BarrierHandlerState` state machine transitions. When all channels aligned: `allBarriersReceivedFuture.complete(null)` and `notifyCheckpoint(barrier)`.\n    - **`CheckpointBarrierTracker.processBarrier()`** (`CheckpointBarrierTracker.java:94`) — For at-least-once: never blocks channels; tracks `CheckpointBarrierCount` per checkpoint ID; when count reaches target calls `triggerCheckpointOnAligned()` → `notifyCheckpoint(barrier)`.\n\n12. **Downstream task checkpoint trigger**: `CheckpointBarrierHandler.notifyCheckpoint()` (`CheckpointBarrierHandler.java:147`) → `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier(checkpointMetaData, options, metrics)` → `StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` → `performCheckpoint()` → same `subtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState()` flow as step 8 (recursively propagating the barrier further downstream).\n\n13. **State snapshot** (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:725`):\n    - `takeSnapshotSync()` calls `operatorChain.snapshotState(snapshotFutures, ...)` which calls each operator's `snapshotState()` synchronously (for RocksDB incremental) or initiates async writes.\n    - `finishAndReportAsync()` creates an `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` submitted to `asyncOperationsThreadPool` which waits for all `OperatorSnapshotFutures` to complete.\n\n14. **ACK sent to JobManager**: `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` upon completion calls `env.acknowledgeCheckpoint(checkpointId, checkpointMetrics, taskStateSnapshot)` → `RuntimeEnvironment.acknowledgeCheckpoint()` → sends `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC message to the JobManager.\n\n15. **Coordinator receives ACK**: `CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()` (`CheckpointCoordinator.java:1210`) — acquires coordinator lock, calls `checkpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionId, subtaskState, metrics)` (`PendingCheckpoint.java`).\n\n16. **Completion check**: If `checkpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()` (tasks + operator coordinators + master states all acked), calls `completePendingCheckpoint(checkpoint)`.\n\n17. **Checkpoint finalization** (`CheckpointCoordinator.java:1365`):\n    - `finalizeCheckpoint(pendingCheckpoint)` serializes metadata and creates `CompletedCheckpoint`\n    - `addCompletedCheckpointToStoreAndSubsumeOldest(...)` persists to `CompletedCheckpointStore` (ZooKeeper/filesystem HA)\n    - `onCompletionPromise.complete(completedCheckpoint)` — resolves the future returned from `triggerCheckpoint()`\n    - `sendAcknowledgeMessages(tasksToCommitTo, checkpointId, ...)` — notifies all tasks of checkpoint completion so they can commit (e.g., Kafka sink 2PC commit)\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns\n\n**Two-Phase Commit (2PC)**:\nThe entire checkpoint protocol follows a distributed 2PC pattern. Phase 1 (prepare/vote): coordinator triggers, tasks snapshot state and send ACK. Phase 2 (commit): once all ACKs received, coordinator finalizes `CompletedCheckpoint` and broadcasts `notifyCheckpointComplete` to all tasks (who then commit external sinks). Abort is possible if any task declines or times out.\n\n**State Machine for Barrier Handling**:\n`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` uses `BarrierHandlerState` as a strategy/state-machine pattern. States include `WaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingCollectingBarriers`, `CollectingBarriers` etc. — each implementing `barrierReceived()`, `announcementReceived()`, and `alignedCheckpointTimeout()` transitions. This enables the \"alternating checkpoint\" mode which dynamically switches between aligned and unaligned based on alignment timeout.\n\n**Observer / Listener**:\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` holds a reference to `CheckpointableTask toNotifyOnCheckpoint`. When barriers are complete, it calls `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` — a push notification to the task. Similarly, `CheckpointCoordinator` acts as the observer for `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` messages.\n\n**Async Pipeline**:\n`startTriggeringCheckpoint()` is structured as a `CompletableFuture` pipeline: plan → ID allocation → PendingCheckpoint → storage location initialization → coordinator checkpoints → master hooks → `triggerCheckpointRequest()`. This avoids blocking the checkpoint timer thread.\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility |\n|---|---|\n| `CheckpointCoordinator` | Central orchestrator (JobManager side): triggers, tracks pending checkpoints, collects ACKs, finalizes/aborts, manages timeout |\n| `PendingCheckpoint` | Mutable in-flight checkpoint state: tracks which tasks/coordinators have not yet acknowledged |\n| `CompletedCheckpoint` | Immutable record of a successful checkpoint with all state handles; persisted to HA store |\n| `Execution` | Proxy for a running task; dispatches checkpoint RPC via `TaskManagerGateway` |\n| `StreamTask` | Task runtime; receives trigger RPC, delegates to `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`; receives barrier callbacks from `CheckpointBarrierHandler` |\n| `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl` | Task-local coordinator: broadcasts barrier, orchestrates operator snapshot, launches async finalization |\n| `CheckpointedInputGate` | Input gate wrapper that intercepts checkpoint barrier events from network |\n| `CheckpointBarrierHandler` (abstract) | Reacts to barriers, manages alignment timing, notifies task when checkpoint can be taken |\n| `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` | Exactly-once barrier handler (aligned or unaligned); blocks channels during alignment; state machine driven |\n| `CheckpointBarrierTracker` | At-least-once barrier handler; tracks multiple concurrent checkpoints without blocking |\n| `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` | Off-thread async snapshot completion; sends ACK to JobManager upon success |\n\n### Data Flow Description\n\n```\nJobManager timer\n    → CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()\n    → [creates PendingCheckpoint, calculates CheckpointPlan]\n    → [triggers OperatorCoordinator checkpoints + master hooks]\n    → Execution.triggerCheckpoint() [for each source task]\n        → TaskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint() [RPC]\n            → StreamTask.triggerCheckpointAsync()\n                → SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()\n                    → operatorChain.broadcastEvent(CheckpointBarrier)\n                        → [barrier flows through output buffers to network]\n                    → takeSnapshotSync() [operator state snapshot]\n                    → finishAndReportAsync() → AsyncCheckpointRunnable\n                        → env.acknowledgeCheckpoint() [RPC back to JM]\n\n[Barrier flows through network channels to downstream tasks]\n    → CheckpointedInputGate intercepts CheckpointBarrier\n        → CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()\n            [Aligned / SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler]:\n                → waits for barriers from ALL input channels\n                → blocks channels that have sent barrier (backpressure)\n                → when all received: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n                    → StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()\n                        → same snapshot flow as above\n            [At-least-once / CheckpointBarrierTracker]:\n                → counts received barriers per checkpoint ID\n                → does NOT block channels\n                → when all received: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n\nJobManager receives AcknowledgeCheckpoint messages:\n    → CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()\n        → PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()\n        → if isFullyAcknowledged():\n            → completePendingCheckpoint()\n                → finalizeCheckpoint() → CompletedCheckpoint\n                → CompletedCheckpointStore.addCheckpointAndSubsumeOldest()\n                → sendAcknowledgeMessages() [notify tasks: commit external state]\n```\n\n### Interface Contracts Between Components\n\n- **`CheckpointableTask`** (implemented by `StreamTask`): the interface `CheckpointBarrierHandler` uses to notify tasks — `triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` and `abortCheckpointOnBarrier()`.\n- **`TaskManagerGateway`**: RPC interface between Execution (coordinator side) and remote task; carries `triggerCheckpoint()`.\n- **`CheckpointCoordinatorGateway`**: RPC interface on JobManager for tasks to send `acknowledgeCheckpoint()` and `declineCheckpoint()`.\n- **`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinator`**: interface between `StreamTask` and `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`, exposing `checkpointState()`, `notifyCheckpointComplete()`, `abortCheckpointOnBarrier()`.\n- **`BarrierHandlerState`**: strategy interface used by `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` for state transitions; implementations encapsulate alignment logic.\n\n### Aligned vs Unaligned Checkpoint Barrier Handling\n\n**`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (aligned mode)**:\n- Created via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.aligned(...)` with initial state `WaitingForFirstBarrier`.\n- On first barrier: starts alignment timer, blocks the channel (backpressure). Records it in `alignedChannels`.\n- Subsequent channels: blocks each as their barrier arrives.\n- When `alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`: calls `notifyCheckpoint()` → task snapshots state with no in-flight records crossing the barrier.\n- Guarantees exactly-once: no records between pre- and post-barrier data mix.\n\n**`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (unaligned mode)**:\n- Created via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.unaligned(...)` with state `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`.\n- On first barrier announcement: immediately triggers checkpoint (calls `notifyCheckpoint`). Does NOT block channels.\n- In-flight channel buffers are snapshotted as part of channel state (via `ChannelStateWriter`) — records in-transit are included in the checkpoint.\n- Much lower latency under backpressure since channels never stall.\n\n**Alternating mode** (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.alternating(...)`):\n- Starts as aligned but if alignment exceeds `alignedCheckpointTimeout`, converts to unaligned via `alignedCheckpointTimeout()` state transition.\n\n**`CheckpointBarrierTracker`** (at-least-once):\n- Never blocks channels; maintains a queue of `CheckpointBarrierCount` objects tracking how many channels have sent each checkpoint's barrier.\n- Supports multiple concurrent in-flight checkpoints (up to `MAX_CHECKPOINTS_TO_TRACK = 50`).\n- When all channels for a checkpoint ID have been seen, fires `notifyCheckpoint()`.\n- Does not prevent records from mixing across checkpoint boundaries → at-least-once semantics only.\n\n### PendingCheckpoint Lifecycle\n\n1. **Created**: `CheckpointCoordinator.createPendingCheckpoint()` — sets `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` from `checkpointPlan.getTasksToWaitFor()`, schedules timeout via `CheckpointCanceller`.\n2. **Progressing**: Each `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` message calls `PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionId, subtaskState, metrics)` — moves task from `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` to `acknowledgedTasks`, stores `OperatorSubtaskState` in `operatorStates` map.\n3. **Fully acknowledged**: `isFullyAcknowledged()` = `areTasksFullyAcknowledged() && areCoordinatorsFullyAcknowledged() && areMasterStatesFullyAcknowledged()`. Triggers `completePendingCheckpoint()`.\n4. **Completed**: Converted to `CompletedCheckpoint` via `finalizeCheckpoint()`, which writes checkpoint metadata to storage. Removed from `pendingCheckpoints` map.\n5. **Discarded/Aborted**: Via `abortPendingCheckpoint()` on timeout (`CheckpointCanceller`) or task decline (`DeclineCheckpoint` message) — canceller handle is used to cancel the timeout, state handles are discarded, `onCompletionPromise` is failed.\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nFlink checkpoint coordination implements a distributed two-phase commit: the `CheckpointCoordinator` (JobManager) triggers checkpoints by sending RPC calls to source tasks via `Execution.triggerCheckpoint()` → `TaskManagerGateway`, which causes each `StreamTask` to broadcast a `CheckpointBarrier` downstream through its output buffers via `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`. Downstream tasks receive barriers through `CheckpointedInputGate`, with `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` providing exactly-once semantics by blocking channels until all barriers are aligned (or triggering immediately for unaligned checkpoints), while `CheckpointBarrierTracker` provides at-least-once semantics without blocking. Each task snapshots operator state asynchronously and sends an `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC back to `CheckpointCoordinator`, which tracks progress in `PendingCheckpoint`; once all tasks and operator coordinators have acknowledged, `completePendingCheckpoint()` finalizes the `CompletedCheckpoint` in the HA store and broadcasts completion notifications so external sinks can commit their transactions.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4826,"cache_read_input_tokens":70111,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":4826,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":9,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b9064414-21b5-46ce-8772-4b8512fa54ba","uuid":"9acfd392-6da2-4a83-9c97-93104cfee632"}

`chooseRequestToExecute(request).ifPresent(this::startTriggeringCheckpoint)` queues or immediately executes the trigger through `CheckpointRequestDecider`.\n\n3. **Plan calculation**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:642` — `checkpointPlanCalculator.calculateCheckpointPlan()` (`DefaultCheckpointPlanCalculator`) determines `tasksToTrigger` (sources/operators with no inputs), `tasksToWaitFor` (all tasks needing to ack), and `tasksToCommitTo`.\n\n4. **PendingCheckpoint creation**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:901` — `createPendingCheckpoint(...)` instantiates `PendingCheckpoint` with `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` from the plan, schedules a `CheckpointCanceller` timeout, inserts into `pendingCheckpoints` map.\n\n5. **Coordinator & master hook snapshots**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:708,736` — `OperatorCoordinatorCheckpoints.triggerAndAcknowledgeAllCoordinatorCheckpointsWithCompletion(...)` and `snapshotMasterState(checkpoint)` run asynchronously; combined into `masterTriggerCompletionPromise` before dispatching to tasks.\n\n6. **RPC dispatch to source tasks**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:836-867` — `triggerTasks()` iterates `checkpoint.getCheckpointPlan().getTasksToTrigger()` and calls `execution.triggerCheckpoint(checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)`.\n\n7. **RPC to TaskManager**: `Execution.java:1096` — `slot.getTaskManagerGateway().triggerCheckpoint(attemptId, jobId, checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)` — actual RPC to the remote TaskManager hosting the task.\n\n8. **Task receives trigger**: `StreamTask.java:1459` — `performCheckpoint()` → `subtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState(checkpointMetaData, checkpointOptions, checkpointMetrics, operatorChain, ...)`.\n\n9. **Barrier broadcast** (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:333,344`):\n   - Step (1): `operatorChain.prepareSnapshotPreBarrier(checkpointId)` — pre-barrier operator hooks\n   - Step (2): `operatorChain.broadcastEvent(new CheckpointBarrier(id, ts, options), isUnaligned)` — injects barrier into all output buffers, flowing to downstream tasks through the network\n\n10. **Barrier reception at downstream task**: `CheckpointedInputGate` intercepts `CheckpointBarrier` arriving from `InputGate` channels and calls `barrierHandler.processBarrier(barrier, channelInfo, false)`.\n\n11. **Barrier alignment / tracking** (two implementations):\n    - **`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()`** (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.java:214`) — Exactly-once: tracks `alignedChannels`; for aligned mode, blocks input channels after their barrier arrives (via `CheckpointableInput`); uses `BarrierHandlerState` for state machine transitions (`barrierReceived()`, `announcementReceived()`, `alignedCheckpointTimeout()`). When all channels aligned (`alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`): completes `allBarriersReceivedFuture`, calls `notifyCheckpoint(barrier)`.\n    - **`CheckpointBarrierTracker.processBarrier()`** (`CheckpointBarrierTracker.java:94`) — At-least-once: never blocks channels; maintains `ArrayDeque<CheckpointBarrierCount>` per checkpoint; when `markChannelAligned()` count reaches target, calls `triggerCheckpointOnAligned()` → `notifyCheckpoint(barrier)`.\n\n12. **Downstream task checkpoint trigger**: `CheckpointBarrierHandler.notifyCheckpoint()` (`CheckpointBarrierHandler.java:147`) → `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier(checkpointMetaData, options, metrics)` → `StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` (`StreamTask.java:1396`) → `performCheckpoint()` → same `subtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()` flow, which in turn broadcasts the barrier further downstream (recursive propagation).\n\n13. **State snapshot** (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:725`):\n    - `takeSnapshotSync()` calls `operatorChain.snapshotState(snapshotFutures, ...)` — each operator's `snapshotState()` runs synchronously for the metadata; actual state writing may be async.\n    - `finishAndReportAsync()` (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:690`) creates `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` submitted to `asyncOperationsThreadPool` which awaits all `OperatorSnapshotFutures`.\n\n14. **ACK sent to JobManager**: `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` upon completion calls `env.acknowledgeCheckpoint(checkpointId, checkpointMetrics, taskStateSnapshot)` → `RuntimeEnvironment.acknowledgeCheckpoint()` → sends `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC message to the JobManager's `CheckpointCoordinatorGateway`.\n\n15. **Coordinator receives ACK**: `CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()` (`CheckpointCoordinator.java:1210`) — acquires coordinator lock, calls `checkpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionId, subtaskState, metrics)` on the `PendingCheckpoint`.\n\n16. **Completion check**: If `checkpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()` (all tasks + operator coordinators + master states acked), calls `completePendingCheckpoint(checkpoint)`.\n\n17. **Checkpoint finalization** (`CheckpointCoordinator.java:1365`):\n    - `finalizeCheckpoint(pendingCheckpoint)` serializes metadata, creates `CompletedCheckpoint`\n    - `addCompletedCheckpointToStoreAndSubsumeOldest(...)` persists to `CompletedCheckpointStore` (ZooKeeper or filesystem HA store); older checkpoints may be subsumed and discarded\n    - `onCompletionPromise.complete(completedCheckpoint)` — resolves the `CompletableFuture<CompletedCheckpoint>` returned from `triggerCheckpoint()`\n    - `sendAcknowledgeMessages(tasksToCommitTo, checkpointId, ...)` — notifies all committing tasks so they can call `notifyCheckpointComplete()` (e.g., Kafka sink 2PC commit)\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns\n\n**Distributed Two-Phase Commit (2PC)**:\nThe checkpoint protocol mirrors 2PC exactly. Phase 1 (prepare): coordinator sends trigger RPCs, tasks snapshot state and send ACK. Phase 2 (commit): once all ACKs received, coordinator persists `CompletedCheckpoint` and broadcasts `notifyCheckpointComplete` to all tasks, which commit external state (e.g., Kafka offsets). Abort is triggered by task declines, failures, or timeout.\n\n**State Machine for Barrier Handling**:\n`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` uses `BarrierHandlerState` as a strategy/state-machine. States (`WaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`, `CollectingBarriers`) implement `barrierReceived()`, `announcementReceived()`, and `alignedCheckpointTimeout()` transitions. This enables the \"alternating checkpoint\" mode that dynamically switches between aligned and unaligned on alignment timeout.\n\n**Observer / Listener**:\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` holds `CheckpointableTask toNotifyOnCheckpoint`. When barriers complete, it calls `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()`. `CheckpointCoordinator` observes `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC messages from all tasks.\n\n**Async Pipeline (CompletableFuture chaining)**:\n`startTriggeringCheckpoint()` is a `CompletableFuture` pipeline: plan calculation → ID allocation → `PendingCheckpoint` creation → storage location init → coordinator checkpoints → master hooks → `triggerCheckpointRequest()`. Avoids blocking the checkpoint timer thread.\n\n**Template Method**:\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` (abstract) defines the notification protocol (`notifyCheckpoint`, `notifyAbort`, alignment tracking) while leaving `processBarrier()`, `processBarrierAnnouncement()`, and `isCheckpointPending()` abstract for `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` and `CheckpointBarrierTracker`.\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility |\n|---|---|\n| `CheckpointCoordinator` | Central orchestrator (JobManager): triggers, tracks pending, collects ACKs, finalizes/aborts, manages timeout |\n| `PendingCheckpoint` | Mutable in-flight state: tracks un-acked tasks/coordinators/master states, accumulates `OperatorSubtaskState` |\n| `CompletedCheckpoint` | Immutable record of a successful checkpoint with all state handles; persisted to HA store |\n| `Execution` | Proxy for a running task; dispatches checkpoint RPC via `TaskManagerGateway` |\n| `StreamTask` | Task runtime; receives trigger RPC, delegates to `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`; receives barrier callbacks |\n| `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl` | Task-local coordinator: broadcasts barrier, orchestrates operator snapshot, launches async finalization |\n| `CheckpointedInputGate` | Input gate wrapper intercepting `CheckpointBarrier` events from the network |\n| `CheckpointBarrierHandler` (abstract) | Reacts to barriers, manages alignment timing, notifies task when checkpoint can proceed |\n| `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` | Exactly-once barrier handler (aligned/unaligned/alternating); state machine driven |\n| `CheckpointBarrierTracker` | At-least-once barrier handler; tracks multiple concurrent checkpoints without blocking |\n| `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` | Off-thread async snapshot completion; sends ACK to JobManager upon success |\n\n### Data Flow\n\n```\nJobManager timer\n    → CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()\n    → [creates PendingCheckpoint, CheckpointPlan]\n    → [triggers OperatorCoordinator checkpoints + master hooks]\n    → Execution.triggerCheckpoint() [for each source task]\n        → TaskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint() [RPC]\n            → StreamTask.performCheckpoint()\n                → SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()\n                    → operatorChain.prepareSnapshotPreBarrier()\n                    → operatorChain.broadcastEvent(CheckpointBarrier)\n                        → [barrier flows downstream through network buffers]\n                    → takeSnapshotSync() → operatorChain.snapshotState()\n                    → finishAndReportAsync() → AsyncCheckpointRunnable\n                        → env.acknowledgeCheckpoint() [RPC → JobManager]\n\n[Barrier arrives at downstream task via CheckpointedInputGate]\n    → CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()\n        [SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler / aligned]:\n            → blocks channel, records in alignedChannels\n            → when all channels aligned: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n                → StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()\n                    → same snapshot + broadcast + ACK flow\n        [SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler / unaligned]:\n            → triggers immediately on first barrier (announcement)\n            → snapshots in-flight channel buffers via ChannelStateWriter\n        [CheckpointBarrierTracker / at-least-once]:\n            → counts barriers, no blocking\n            → when all seen: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n\nJobManager collects AcknowledgeCheckpoint messages:\n    → CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()\n        → PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()\n        → if isFullyAcknowledged():\n            → completePendingCheckpoint()\n                → finalizeCheckpoint() → CompletedCheckpoint\n                → CompletedCheckpointStore.addCheckpoint()\n                → sendAcknowledgeMessages() [tasks commit external state]\n```\n\n### Aligned vs Unaligned Checkpoint Barrier Handling\n\n**`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (aligned mode)**:\n- Created via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.aligned(...)` with initial state `WaitingForFirstBarrier`.\n- On first barrier from any channel: starts alignment timer, records channel in `alignedChannels`, blocks that channel (backpressure via `CheckpointableInput`).\n- Subsequent barriers from other channels: each is blocked in turn.\n- When `alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`: calls `notifyCheckpoint()`. Task snapshots state with a clean cut — no records cross the barrier boundary.\n- Guarantees exactly-once: pre-barrier and post-barrier records are never mixed.\n\n**`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (unaligned mode)**:\n- Created via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.unaligned(...)` with state `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`.\n- On first barrier announcement: immediately triggers checkpoint (`notifyCheckpoint()`). Does NOT block channels.\n- In-flight buffers in all channels are snapshotted as channel state via `ChannelStateWriter` — records in transit are included in the checkpoint.\n- Much lower checkpoint latency under backpressure since no channel stalling occurs.\n\n**Alternating mode** (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.alternating(...)`):\n- Starts as aligned but converts to unaligned if `alignedCheckpointTimeout` elapses, via `alignedCheckpointTimeout()` state transition.\n\n**`CheckpointBarrierTracker`** (at-least-once):\n- Never blocks channels; maintains `ArrayDeque<CheckpointBarrierCount>` tracking received barrier count per checkpoint ID.\n- Supports multiple concurrent in-flight checkpoints (up to `MAX_CHECKPOINTS_TO_TRACK = 50`).\n- When all channels for a checkpoint ID have sent their barrier, fires `triggerCheckpointOnAligned()` → `notifyCheckpoint()`.\n- Does not prevent records from flowing across the checkpoint boundary → at-least-once semantics only.\n\n### PendingCheckpoint Lifecycle and Ack-Based Completion Protocol\n\n1. **Created**: `createPendingCheckpoint()` — `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` populated from `checkpointPlan.getTasksToWaitFor()`; timeout canceller scheduled.\n2. **Progressing**: Each `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` message → `PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionId, subtaskState, metrics)` moves task from `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` to `acknowledgedTasks`, stores `OperatorSubtaskState` in `operatorStates` map. Returns `TaskAcknowledgeResult.SUCCESS` (or `DUPLICATE`/`UNKNOWN`/`DISCARDED`).\n3. **Coordinator acks**: `OperatorCoordinatorCheckpoints` calls `pendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeCoordinatorState()` for each coordinator completing its snapshot; tracked in `notYetAcknowledgedOperatorCoordinators`.\n4. **Master state acks**: `snapshotMasterState()` calls `checkpoint.acknowledgeMasterState(identifier, state)` for each master hook.\n5. **Fully acknowledged**: `isFullyAcknowledged()` = `areTasksFullyAcknowledged() && areCoordinatorsFullyAcknowledged() && areMasterStatesFullyAcknowledged()` → triggers `completePendingCheckpoint()`.\n6. **Completed**: `finalizeCheckpoint()` serializes and persists checkpoint metadata; `PendingCheckpoint` is disposed; `CompletedCheckpoint` added to store and returned.\n7. **Aborted/Discarded**: `abortPendingCheckpoint()` on timeout or task decline — `CheckpointCanceller` fires, state handles discarded, `onCompletionPromise` completed exceptionally, `CancelCheckpointMarker` broadcast to downstream.\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nFlink checkpoint coordination implements a distributed two-phase commit driven by `CheckpointCoordinator` on the JobManager: it triggers checkpoints by sending RPCs to source tasks via `Execution` → `TaskManagerGateway`, which causes each `StreamTask` (via `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`) to broadcast a `CheckpointBarrier` downstream through its output buffers while simultaneously taking an async state snapshot. Downstream tasks receive barriers through `CheckpointedInputGate` and `CheckpointBarrierHandler` — `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` provides exactly-once by blocking channels until all barriers align (or triggers immediately for unaligned checkpoints with in-flight buffer capture), while `CheckpointBarrierTracker` provides at-least-once by counting barriers without blocking. Once all tasks send `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPCs, `CheckpointCoordinator` transitions the `PendingCheckpoint` to a `CompletedCheckpoint` persisted in the HA store and broadcasts completion notifications so external sinks can commit their transactions, completing the 2PC protocol.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":355,"cache_read_input_tokens":80945,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":355,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b9064414-21b5-46ce-8772-4b8512fa54ba","uuid":"c1055ed0-77f0-4b24-9c41-80f780abb1da"}

savepoints), delegates to `triggerCheckpointFromCheckpointThread()`.\n\n2. **Request routing**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:626` — `chooseRequestToExecute(request).ifPresent(this::startTriggeringCheckpoint)` queues or immediately executes the trigger through `CheckpointRequestDecider`.\n\n3. **Plan calculation**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:642` — `checkpointPlanCalculator.calculateCheckpointPlan()` (`DefaultCheckpointPlanCalculator`) determines `tasksToTrigger` (sources/operators with no inputs), `tasksToWaitFor` (all tasks needing to ack), and `tasksToCommitTo`.\n\n4. **PendingCheckpoint creation**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:901` — `createPendingCheckpoint(...)` instantiates `PendingCheckpoint` with `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` from the plan, schedules a `CheckpointCanceller` timeout, inserts into `pendingCheckpoints` map.\n\n5. **Coordinator & master hook snapshots**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:708,736` — `OperatorCoordinatorCheckpoints.triggerAndAcknowledgeAllCoordinatorCheckpointsWithCompletion(...)` and `snapshotMasterState(checkpoint)` run asynchronously; combined into `masterTriggerCompletionPromise` before dispatching to tasks.\n\n6. **RPC dispatch to source tasks**: `CheckpointCoordinator.java:836-867` — `triggerTasks()` iterates `checkpoint.getCheckpointPlan().getTasksToTrigger()` and calls `execution.triggerCheckpoint(checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)`.\n\n7. **RPC to TaskManager**: `Execution.java:1096` — `slot.getTaskManagerGateway().triggerCheckpoint(attemptId, jobId, checkpointId, timestamp, checkpointOptions)` — actual RPC to the remote TaskManager hosting the task.\n\n8. **Task receives trigger**: `StreamTask.java:1459` — `performCheckpoint()` → `subtaskCheckpointCoordinator.checkpointState(checkpointMetaData, checkpointOptions, checkpointMetrics, operatorChain, ...)`.\n\n9. **Barrier broadcast** (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:333,344`):\n   - Step (1): `operatorChain.prepareSnapshotPreBarrier(checkpointId)` — pre-barrier operator hooks\n   - Step (2): `operatorChain.broadcastEvent(new CheckpointBarrier(id, ts, options), isUnaligned)` — injects barrier into all output buffers, flowing to downstream tasks through the network\n\n10. **Barrier reception at downstream task**: `CheckpointedInputGate` intercepts `CheckpointBarrier` arriving from `InputGate` channels and calls `barrierHandler.processBarrier(barrier, channelInfo, false)`.\n\n11. **Barrier alignment / tracking** (two implementations):\n    - **`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()`** (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.java:214`) — Exactly-once: tracks `alignedChannels`; for aligned mode, blocks input channels after their barrier arrives (via `CheckpointableInput`); uses `BarrierHandlerState` for state machine transitions (`barrierReceived()`, `announcementReceived()`, `alignedCheckpointTimeout()`). When all channels aligned (`alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`): completes `allBarriersReceivedFuture`, calls `notifyCheckpoint(barrier)`.\n    - **`CheckpointBarrierTracker.processBarrier()`** (`CheckpointBarrierTracker.java:94`) — At-least-once: never blocks channels; maintains `ArrayDeque<CheckpointBarrierCount>` per checkpoint; when `markChannelAligned()` count reaches target, calls `triggerCheckpointOnAligned()` → `notifyCheckpoint(barrier)`.\n\n12. **Downstream task checkpoint trigger**: `CheckpointBarrierHandler.notifyCheckpoint()` (`CheckpointBarrierHandler.java:147`) → `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier(checkpointMetaData, options, metrics)` → `StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()` (`StreamTask.java:1396`) → `performCheckpoint()` → same `subtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()` flow, which in turn broadcasts the barrier further downstream (recursive propagation).\n\n13. **State snapshot** (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:725`):\n    - `takeSnapshotSync()` calls `operatorChain.snapshotState(snapshotFutures, ...)` — each operator's `snapshotState()` runs synchronously for the metadata; actual state writing may be async.\n    - `finishAndReportAsync()` (`SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.java:690`) creates `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` submitted to `asyncOperationsThreadPool` which awaits all `OperatorSnapshotFutures`.\n\n14. **ACK sent to JobManager**: `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` upon completion calls `env.acknowledgeCheckpoint(checkpointId, checkpointMetrics, taskStateSnapshot)` → `RuntimeEnvironment.acknowledgeCheckpoint()` → sends `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC message to the JobManager's `CheckpointCoordinatorGateway`.\n\n15. **Coordinator receives ACK**: `CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()` (`CheckpointCoordinator.java:1210`) — acquires coordinator lock, calls `checkpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionId, subtaskState, metrics)` on the `PendingCheckpoint`.\n\n16. **Completion check**: If `checkpoint.isFullyAcknowledged()` (all tasks + operator coordinators + master states acked), calls `completePendingCheckpoint(checkpoint)`.\n\n17. **Checkpoint finalization** (`CheckpointCoordinator.java:1365`):\n    - `finalizeCheckpoint(pendingCheckpoint)` serializes metadata, creates `CompletedCheckpoint`\n    - `addCompletedCheckpointToStoreAndSubsumeOldest(...)` persists to `CompletedCheckpointStore` (ZooKeeper or filesystem HA store); older checkpoints may be subsumed and discarded\n    - `onCompletionPromise.complete(completedCheckpoint)` — resolves the `CompletableFuture<CompletedCheckpoint>` returned from `triggerCheckpoint()`\n    - `sendAcknowledgeMessages(tasksToCommitTo, checkpointId, ...)` — notifies all committing tasks so they can call `notifyCheckpointComplete()` (e.g., Kafka sink 2PC commit)\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns\n\n**Distributed Two-Phase Commit (2PC)**:\nThe checkpoint protocol mirrors 2PC exactly. Phase 1 (prepare): coordinator sends trigger RPCs, tasks snapshot state and send ACK. Phase 2 (commit): once all ACKs received, coordinator persists `CompletedCheckpoint` and broadcasts `notifyCheckpointComplete` to all tasks, which commit external state (e.g., Kafka offsets). Abort is triggered by task declines, failures, or timeout.\n\n**State Machine for Barrier Handling**:\n`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` uses `BarrierHandlerState` as a strategy/state-machine. States (`WaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrier`, `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`, `CollectingBarriers`) implement `barrierReceived()`, `announcementReceived()`, and `alignedCheckpointTimeout()` transitions. This enables the \"alternating checkpoint\" mode that dynamically switches between aligned and unaligned on alignment timeout.\n\n**Observer / Listener**:\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` holds `CheckpointableTask toNotifyOnCheckpoint`. When barriers complete, it calls `toNotifyOnCheckpoint.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()`. `CheckpointCoordinator` observes `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPC messages from all tasks.\n\n**Async Pipeline (CompletableFuture chaining)**:\n`startTriggeringCheckpoint()` is a `CompletableFuture` pipeline: plan calculation → ID allocation → `PendingCheckpoint` creation → storage location init → coordinator checkpoints → master hooks → `triggerCheckpointRequest()`. Avoids blocking the checkpoint timer thread.\n\n**Template Method**:\n`CheckpointBarrierHandler` (abstract) defines the notification protocol (`notifyCheckpoint`, `notifyAbort`, alignment tracking) while leaving `processBarrier()`, `processBarrierAnnouncement()`, and `isCheckpointPending()` abstract for `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` and `CheckpointBarrierTracker`.\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility |\n|---|---|\n| `CheckpointCoordinator` | Central orchestrator (JobManager): triggers, tracks pending, collects ACKs, finalizes/aborts, manages timeout |\n| `PendingCheckpoint` | Mutable in-flight state: tracks un-acked tasks/coordinators/master states, accumulates `OperatorSubtaskState` |\n| `CompletedCheckpoint` | Immutable record of a successful checkpoint with all state handles; persisted to HA store |\n| `Execution` | Proxy for a running task; dispatches checkpoint RPC via `TaskManagerGateway` |\n| `StreamTask` | Task runtime; receives trigger RPC, delegates to `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`; receives barrier callbacks |\n| `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl` | Task-local coordinator: broadcasts barrier, orchestrates operator snapshot, launches async finalization |\n| `CheckpointedInputGate` | Input gate wrapper intercepting `CheckpointBarrier` events from the network |\n| `CheckpointBarrierHandler` (abstract) | Reacts to barriers, manages alignment timing, notifies task when checkpoint can proceed |\n| `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` | Exactly-once barrier handler (aligned/unaligned/alternating); state machine driven |\n| `CheckpointBarrierTracker` | At-least-once barrier handler; tracks multiple concurrent checkpoints without blocking |\n| `AsyncCheckpointRunnable` | Off-thread async snapshot completion; sends ACK to JobManager upon success |\n\n### Data Flow\n\n```\nJobManager timer\n    → CheckpointCoordinator.triggerCheckpoint()\n    → [creates PendingCheckpoint, CheckpointPlan]\n    → [triggers OperatorCoordinator checkpoints + master hooks]\n    → Execution.triggerCheckpoint() [for each source task]\n        → TaskManagerGateway.triggerCheckpoint() [RPC]\n            → StreamTask.performCheckpoint()\n                → SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl.checkpointState()\n                    → operatorChain.prepareSnapshotPreBarrier()\n                    → operatorChain.broadcastEvent(CheckpointBarrier)\n                        → [barrier flows downstream through network buffers]\n                    → takeSnapshotSync() → operatorChain.snapshotState()\n                    → finishAndReportAsync() → AsyncCheckpointRunnable\n                        → env.acknowledgeCheckpoint() [RPC → JobManager]\n\n[Barrier arrives at downstream task via CheckpointedInputGate]\n    → CheckpointBarrierHandler.processBarrier()\n        [SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler / aligned]:\n            → blocks channel, records in alignedChannels\n            → when all channels aligned: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n                → StreamTask.triggerCheckpointOnBarrier()\n                    → same snapshot + broadcast + ACK flow\n        [SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler / unaligned]:\n            → triggers immediately on first barrier (announcement)\n            → snapshots in-flight channel buffers via ChannelStateWriter\n        [CheckpointBarrierTracker / at-least-once]:\n            → counts barriers, no blocking\n            → when all seen: notifyCheckpoint(barrier)\n\nJobManager collects AcknowledgeCheckpoint messages:\n    → CheckpointCoordinator.receiveAcknowledgeMessage()\n        → PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask()\n        → if isFullyAcknowledged():\n            → completePendingCheckpoint()\n                → finalizeCheckpoint() → CompletedCheckpoint\n                → CompletedCheckpointStore.addCheckpoint()\n                → sendAcknowledgeMessages() [tasks commit external state]\n```\n\n### Aligned vs Unaligned Checkpoint Barrier Handling\n\n**`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (aligned mode)**:\n- Created via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.aligned(...)` with initial state `WaitingForFirstBarrier`.\n- On first barrier from any channel: starts alignment timer, records channel in `alignedChannels`, blocks that channel (backpressure via `CheckpointableInput`).\n- Subsequent barriers from other channels: each is blocked in turn.\n- When `alignedChannels.size() == targetChannelCount`: calls `notifyCheckpoint()`. Task snapshots state with a clean cut — no records cross the barrier boundary.\n- Guarantees exactly-once: pre-barrier and post-barrier records are never mixed.\n\n**`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` (unaligned mode)**:\n- Created via `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.unaligned(...)` with state `AlternatingWaitingForFirstBarrierUnaligned`.\n- On first barrier announcement: immediately triggers checkpoint (`notifyCheckpoint()`). Does NOT block channels.\n- In-flight buffers in all channels are snapshotted as channel state via `ChannelStateWriter` — records in transit are included in the checkpoint.\n- Much lower checkpoint latency under backpressure since no channel stalling occurs.\n\n**Alternating mode** (`SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler.alternating(...)`):\n- Starts as aligned but converts to unaligned if `alignedCheckpointTimeout` elapses, via `alignedCheckpointTimeout()` state transition.\n\n**`CheckpointBarrierTracker`** (at-least-once):\n- Never blocks channels; maintains `ArrayDeque<CheckpointBarrierCount>` tracking received barrier count per checkpoint ID.\n- Supports multiple concurrent in-flight checkpoints (up to `MAX_CHECKPOINTS_TO_TRACK = 50`).\n- When all channels for a checkpoint ID have sent their barrier, fires `triggerCheckpointOnAligned()` → `notifyCheckpoint()`.\n- Does not prevent records from flowing across the checkpoint boundary → at-least-once semantics only.\n\n### PendingCheckpoint Lifecycle and Ack-Based Completion Protocol\n\n1. **Created**: `createPendingCheckpoint()` — `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` populated from `checkpointPlan.getTasksToWaitFor()`; timeout canceller scheduled.\n2. **Progressing**: Each `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` message → `PendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeTask(executionId, subtaskState, metrics)` moves task from `notYetAcknowledgedTasks` to `acknowledgedTasks`, stores `OperatorSubtaskState` in `operatorStates` map. Returns `TaskAcknowledgeResult.SUCCESS` (or `DUPLICATE`/`UNKNOWN`/`DISCARDED`).\n3. **Coordinator acks**: `OperatorCoordinatorCheckpoints` calls `pendingCheckpoint.acknowledgeCoordinatorState()` for each coordinator completing its snapshot; tracked in `notYetAcknowledgedOperatorCoordinators`.\n4. **Master state acks**: `snapshotMasterState()` calls `checkpoint.acknowledgeMasterState(identifier, state)` for each master hook.\n5. **Fully acknowledged**: `isFullyAcknowledged()` = `areTasksFullyAcknowledged() && areCoordinatorsFullyAcknowledged() && areMasterStatesFullyAcknowledged()` → triggers `completePendingCheckpoint()`.\n6. **Completed**: `finalizeCheckpoint()` serializes and persists checkpoint metadata; `PendingCheckpoint` is disposed; `CompletedCheckpoint` added to store and returned.\n7. **Aborted/Discarded**: `abortPendingCheckpoint()` on timeout or task decline — `CheckpointCanceller` fires, state handles discarded, `onCompletionPromise` completed exceptionally, `CancelCheckpointMarker` broadcast to downstream.\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nFlink checkpoint coordination implements a distributed two-phase commit driven by `CheckpointCoordinator` on the JobManager: it triggers checkpoints by sending RPCs to source tasks via `Execution` → `TaskManagerGateway`, which causes each `StreamTask` (via `SubtaskCheckpointCoordinatorImpl`) to broadcast a `CheckpointBarrier` downstream through its output buffers while simultaneously taking an async state snapshot. Downstream tasks receive barriers through `CheckpointedInputGate` and `CheckpointBarrierHandler` — `SingleCheckpointBarrierHandler` provides exactly-once by blocking channels until all barriers align (or triggers immediately for unaligned checkpoints with in-flight buffer capture), while `CheckpointBarrierTracker` provides at-least-once by counting barriers without blocking. Once all tasks send `AcknowledgeCheckpoint` RPCs, `CheckpointCoordinator` transitions the `PendingCheckpoint` to a `CompletedCheckpoint` persisted in the HA store and broadcasts completion notifications so external sinks can commit their transactions, completing the 2PC protocol.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
